    { 1100525006;3;DataItem;Estimate Line    ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072072;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Line No.);
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  AssumptionLine@1100525000 : Boolean;
                                  SingleSubEstQuantity@1100528600 : Decimal;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF (PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost) AND
                                     (Quantity = 0) AND
                                     NOT PrintZeroLines
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF (PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales) AND
                                     ("Quantity (Sales)" = 0) AND
                                     NOT PrintZeroLines
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  //DP01175.sn
                                  EstimateLineTotal.GET("Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.", "Part Group", Part, "Line No.");
                                  IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
                                    EstimateLineQuantity := Quantity;
                                    EstimateLineHours := Hours;
                                    EstimateLineHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Hours";
                                    EstimateLineLaborAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Labor Amount";
                                    EstimateLineMaterialAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Material Amount";
                                    EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Subc. Amount";
                                    EstimateLinePlantAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Plant Amount";
                                    EstimateLineSundryAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sundry Amount";
                                    EstimateLineAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cost Amount";
                                  END;
                                  IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales THEN BEGIN
                                    EstimateLineQuantity := "Quantity (Sales)";
                                    EstimateLineHours := "Hours (Sales)";
                                    EstimateLineHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Hours (Sales)";
                                    EstimateLineLaborAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Labor Amount (Sales)";
                                    EstimateLineMaterialAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Material Amount (Sales)";
                                    EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Subc. Amount (Sales)";
                                    EstimateLinePlantAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Plant Amount (Sales)";
                                    EstimateLineSundryAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sundry Amount (Sales)";
                                    EstimateLineAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sales Amount";
                                  END;
                                  //DP01175.en

                                  AssumptionLine := FALSE;
                                  IF LineStatusFilter <> '' THEN
                                    AssumptionLine := EstLineInLineStatusFilter("Estimate Line");

                                  EstimateLineAssumption := 0;
                                  IF AssumptionLine THEN BEGIN
                                    //DP01175.sn
                                    EstimateLineLaborAmount := 0;
                                    EstimateLineMaterialAmount := 0;
                                    EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := 0;
                                    EstimateLinePlantAmount := 0;
                                    EstimateLineSundryAmount := 0;
                                    //DP01175.en
                                    EstimateLineAssumption := EstimateLineAmount;
                                  END;

                                  //DP01175.sn
                                  IF CurrencyCode <> Estimate."Currency Code" THEN BEGIN
                                    EstimateLineLaborAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimateLineLaborAmount, FALSE);
                                    EstimateLineMaterialAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimateLineMaterialAmount, FALSE);
                                    EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount, FALSE);
                                    EstimateLinePlantAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimateLinePlantAmount, FALSE);
                                    EstimateLineSundryAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimateLineSundryAmount, FALSE);
                                    EstimateLineAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimateLineAmount, FALSE);
                                    EstimateLineAssumption := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimateLineAssumption, FALSE);
                                  END;
                                  //DP01175.en

                                  IF "Sub-Estimate"."Cumulative Frequency" <> 0 THEN
                                    SingleSubEstQuantity := "Part Quantity" / "Sub-Estimate"."Cumulative Frequency"
                                  ELSE
                                    SingleSubEstQuantity := 0;

                                  CumEstimateLineHours := EstimateLineHours * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineLaborAmount := EstimateLineLaborAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineMaterialAmount := EstimateLineMaterialAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineSubcontractingAmount := EstimateLineSubcontractingAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLinePlantAmount := EstimateLinePlantAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineSundryAmount := EstimateLineSundryAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;
                                  CumEstimateLineAmount := EstimateLineAmount * SingleSubEstQuantity;

                                  IF PartQuantity = 0 THEN
                                    EstimateLineAmount := 0;  //C034086

                                  IF NOT PrintText THEN BEGIN  //db, 07-11-14: C018681
                                    "External Text" := '';
                                    "Internal Text" := '';
                                  END;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part;
               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.),
                            Part Group=FIELD(Part Group),
                            Part=FIELD(Part) }

    { 1100525008;4;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072075;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Estimate No.,Sub-Estimate No.,Part Group,Part,Estimate Line,Recipe Group,Recipe,Line No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT PrintRecipeLines THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF (PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost) AND
                                     (Quantity = 0) AND
                                     NOT PrintZeroRecipeLines
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF (PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales) AND
                                     ("Quantity (Sales)" = 0) AND
                                     NOT PrintZeroRecipeLines
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  EstimateLineTotal.DetermineSurchRcpLine("Estimate Recipe Line", SummarySheet);  //DP01175

                                  IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
                                    RecipeLineQuantity := Quantity;
                                    RecipeLineHours := Hours;
                                    RecipeLineLaborAmount := "Labor Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLineMaterialAmount := "Material Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLineSubcontractingAmount := "Subcontracting Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLinePlantAmount := "Plant Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLineSundryAmount := "Sundry Cost Amount";
                                    RecipeLineAmount := "Cost Amount";
                                  END;
                                  IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales THEN BEGIN
                                    RecipeLineQuantity := "Quantity (Sales)";
                                    RecipeLineHours := "Hours (Sales)";
                                    RecipeLineLaborAmount := "Labor Sales Amount";
                                    RecipeLineMaterialAmount := "Material Sales Amount";
                                    RecipeLineSubcontractingAmount := "Subcontracting Sales Amount";
                                    RecipeLinePlantAmount := "Plant Sales Amount";
                                    RecipeLineSundryAmount := "Sundry Sales Amount";
                                    RecipeLineAmount := "Sales Amount";
                                  END;

                                  //DP01175.sn
                                  IF CurrencyCode <> Estimate."Currency Code" THEN BEGIN
                                    RecipeLineLaborAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(RecipeLineLaborAmount, FALSE);
                                    RecipeLineMaterialAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(RecipeLineMaterialAmount, FALSE);
                                    RecipeLineSubcontractingAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(RecipeLineSubcontractingAmount, FALSE);
                                    RecipeLinePlantAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(RecipeLinePlantAmount, FALSE);
                                    RecipeLineSundryAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(RecipeLineSundryAmount, FALSE);
                                    RecipeLineAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(RecipeLineAmount, FALSE);
                                  END;
                                  //DP01175.en

                                  IF PartQuantity= 0 THEN
                                    RecipeLineAmount := 0;  //C034086

                                  IF NOT PrintText THEN BEGIN
                                    "External Text" := '';
                                    "Internal Text" := '';
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(Estimate No.),
                            Sub-Estimate No.=FIELD(Sub-Estimate No.),
                            Part Group=FIELD(Part Group),
                            Part=FIELD(Part),
                            Estimate Line=FIELD(Line No.) }

    { 1100525009;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012171;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Type)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Type=CONST(Additional Costs));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               "Summary Sheet Line".SETRANGE(Summary, SummarySheet.Summary);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  TotSurchargeAmount := 0;
                                  TotSurchargeHours := 0;
                                  //DP01175.sn
                                  EstimateLineTotal.SummaryLineInFilter(SummarySheet, "Summary Sheet Line", 0, "Summary Sheet Line".Amount, "Summary Sheet Line".Hours, TotSurchargeAmount, TotSurchargeHours);
                                  //DP01175.en
                                  "Summary Sheet Line".Amount += TotSurchargeAmount;
                                  "Summary Sheet Line".Hours += TotSurchargeHours;

                                  TotalEstimate += "Summary Sheet Line".Amount;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Estimate No.=FIELD(No.) }

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF "Estimate Line".GETFILTERS <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', "Estimate Line".TABLECAPTION, "Estimate Line".GETFILTERS));
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineSummarySheet@1100485010(Estimate@1100485001 : Record 11012151;VAR SummerySheet@1100525000 : Record 11012172);
    VAR
      NumSheet@1100525001 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      //first determine the concerning Summary Sheet
      IF IgnoreSummary THEN BEGIN
        CLEAR(SummarySheet);
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF SummaryFilter = '' THEN BEGIN
        //db.sn, 03-07-15: C022055
        SummerySheet.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
        SummerySheet.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", '%1', '');
        IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN
          SummarySheet.SETRANGE("Summary Type", SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost)
        ELSE
          SummarySheet.SETRANGE("Summary Type", SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Sales);
        NumSheet := SummerySheet.COUNT;
        IF NumSheet <> 1 THEN
          ERROR(Text999);
        SummerySheet.FINDFIRST;
        //db.en, 03-07-15: C022055
      END ELSE BEGIN
        SummerySheet.GET(Estimate."No.", SummaryFilter);
      END;

      IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN
        SummarySheet.TESTFIELD("Summary Type", SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Cost)
      ELSE
        SummarySheet.TESTFIELD("Summary Type", SummarySheet."Summary Type"::Sales);

      SummarySheet.CheckAndRefreshSheet;  //db, 17-03-15: C022155
    END;

    PROCEDURE EstLineInLineStatusFilter@1100525001(EstimateLine@1100525000 : Record 11072072) : Boolean;
    VAR
      TempEstimateLine@1100525001 : TEMPORARY Record 11072072;
    BEGIN
      TempEstimateLine := EstimateLine;
      TempEstimateLine.INSERT;

      TempEstimateLine.SETFILTER("Line Status", LineStatusFilter);

      EXIT(TempEstimateLine.FINDFIRST);
    END;

    PROCEDURE EnableFields@1100525002();
    BEGIN
      PrintRecipeLinesEnabled := PrintEstimateLines;
      PrintZeroLinesEnabled := PrintEstimateLines;
      PrintZeroRecipeLinesEnabled := PrintRecipeLines;
      SummaryFilterEnabled := NOT IgnoreSummary;
      PrintAssumptionSeparatelyEnabled := NOT PrintEstimateLines;
      LineStatusFilterEnabled := PrintAssumptionSeparately;
      PrintSurchargeInformationEnabled := NOT IgnoreSummary;
      AggregateTotalsEnabled := (NOT PrintEstimateLines) AND (NOT PrintRecipeLines);  //C032753
    END;

    PROCEDURE LookupSummaryFilter@1100525007();
    VAR
      SummarySheetRec2@1100525000 : Record 11012172;
    BEGIN
      //db, 19-05-11: C015230
      IF "Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No.") <> '' THEN
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
      SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Summary Type", PrintTotalsBasedOn);
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Summary Sheet List",SummarySheetRec2) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN BEGIN
        SummaryFilter := SummarySheetRec2.Summary;
        ValidateSummaryFilter;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ValidateSummaryFilter@1100525006();
    VAR
      SummarySheetRec2@1100525000 : Record 11012172;
    BEGIN
      //db, 19-05-11: C015230
      IF "Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No.") <> '' THEN BEGIN
        //filter on main table only set if report called from estimate; manual change will be evaluated later
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE(Summary, SummaryFilter);
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Summary Type", PrintTotalsBasedOn);
        SummarySheetRec2.FINDSET;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckRelationSummaryEstimate@1100525005();
    VAR
      SummarySheetRec2@1100525000 : Record 11012172;
    BEGIN
      //db, 08-05-11: C015230
      IF IgnoreSummary THEN BEGIN
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF SummaryFilter <>'' THEN BEGIN
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE(Summary,SummaryFilter);
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
        IF NOT SummarySheetRec2.FINDFIRST THEN
          ERROR(Text002);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        SummarySheetRec2.SETRANGE("Estimate No.","Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
        IF NOT SummarySheetRec2.FINDFIRST THEN
          IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Summary Sheet List",SummarySheetRec2) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
            SummaryFilter := SummarySheetRec2.Summary;
      END;

      IF SummarySheetRec2."Sub-Estimate No." <> "Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.") THEN BEGIN
        IF CheckFilterSubEstimate(SummarySheetRec2, "Estimate Line") = FALSE THEN //db, 20-10-09: M16782
          ERROR(Text001);  //db, 08-06-09: M15541
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckFilterSubEstimate@1100525004(VAR SumRec@1100525002 : Record 11012172;VAR EstLineRec@1100525003 : Record 11072072) : Boolean;
    VAR
      SubEstRec@1100525000 : Record 11072074;
      TmpSubEstRec@1100525001 : TEMPORARY Record 11072074;
      SumLineRec@1100525004 : Record 11012171;
      LastFilter@1100525005 : Text[1000];
    BEGIN
      //db, 20-10-09: M16782
      SumLineRec.SETFILTER("Estimate No.", SumRec."Estimate No.");
      SumLineRec.SETFILTER(Summary, SumRec.Summary);
      SumLineRec.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate Filter", '<>%1', '');
      IF SumLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF LastFilter <> SumLineRec."Sub-Estimate Filter" THEN BEGIN
            SubEstRec.SETFILTER("Estimate No.", SumLineRec."Estimate No.");
            SubEstRec.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", SumLineRec."Sub-Estimate Filter");
            IF SubEstRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
              REPEAT
                TmpSubEstRec.COPY(SubEstRec);
                IF TmpSubEstRec.INSERT THEN;
              UNTIL SubEstRec.NEXT = 0;
            END;
          END;
          LastFilter := SumLineRec."Sub-Estimate Filter";
        UNTIL SumLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      SubEstRec.SETFILTER("Estimate No.", EstLineRec.GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
      SubEstRec.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", EstLineRec.GETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No."));
      IF SubEstRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF NOT TmpSubEstRec.GET(SubEstRec."Estimate No.", SubEstRec."Sub-Estimate No.") THEN EXIT(FALSE);
          TmpSubEstRec.DELETE;
        UNTIL SubEstRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      IF TmpSubEstRec.COUNT <> 0 THEN
        EXIT(FALSE)
      ELSE
        EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalculatePartTotals@1100525010();
    VAR
      EstimateLineTotal@1100525000 : Record 11072077;
      EstimateLineTotal2@1100525001 : Record 11072077;
    BEGIN
      //DP01175
      WITH "Estimate Part" DO BEGIN
        //C034086.sn
        InitPartTotals;
        PartQuantity := GetPartQuantity;
        IF PartQuantity = 0 THEN EXIT;
        //C034086.en
        EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
        EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
        CASE Level OF
          1: EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE(Chapter, Chapter);
          2: EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE(Paragraph, Paragraph);
          3: EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE(Part, Part);
        END;
        IF PrintAssumptionSeparately THEN
          EstimateLineTotal.SETFILTER("Line Status", '<>%1', LineStatusFilter);
        IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
          EstimateLineTotal.CALCSUMS(
            "Calc. Hours", "Calc. Cum. Hours",
            "Calc. Labor Amount", "Calc. Cum. Labor Amount",
            "Calc. Material Amount", "Calc. Cum. Material Amount",
            "Calc. Subc. Amount", "Calc. Cum. Subc. Amount",
            "Calc. Plant Amount", "Calc. Cum. Plant Amount",
            "Calc. Sundry Amount", "Calc. Cum. Sundry Amount",
            "Calc. Cost Amount", "Calc. Cum. Cost Amount");
          //
          EstimatePartHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Hours";
          EstimatePartLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Labor Amount";
          EstimatePartMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Material Amount";
          EstimatePartSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Subc. Amount";
          EstimatePartPlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Plant Amount";
          EstimatePartSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sundry Amount";
          EstimatePartAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cost Amount";
          EstimatePartTotal := EstimatePartAmount * "Estimate Part".Quantity;
          //
          EstimatePartCumulativeHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Hours";
          EstimatePartCumulativeLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Labor Amount";
          EstimatePartCumulativeMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Material Amount";
          EstimatePartCumulativeSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Subc. Amount";
          EstimatePartCumulativePlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Plant Amount";
          EstimatePartCumulativeSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sundry Amount";
          EstimatePartCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount";
        END;
        IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales THEN BEGIN
          EstimateLineTotal.CALCSUMS(
            "Calc. Hours (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Hours (Sales)",
            "Calc. Labor Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Labor Amnt (Sales)",
            "Calc. Material Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Mat. Amnt (Sales)",
            "Calc. Subc. Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Subc. Amnt (Sales)",
            "Calc. Plant Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Plant Amnt (Sales)",  //C038483
            "Calc. Sundry Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Sundry Amnt (Sales)",
            "Calc. Sales Amount", "Calc. Cum. Sales Amount");
          //
          EstimatePartHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Hours (Sales)";
          EstimatePartLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Labor Amount (Sales)";
          EstimatePartMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Material Amount (Sales)";
          EstimatePartSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Subc. Amount (Sales)";
          EstimatePartPlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Plant Amount (Sales)";
          EstimatePartSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sundry Amount (Sales)";
          EstimatePartAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sales Amount";
          EstimatePartTotal := EstimatePartAmount * "Estimate Part".Quantity;
          //
          EstimatePartCumulativeHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Hours (Sales)";
          EstimatePartCumulativeLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Labor Amnt (Sales)";
          EstimatePartCumulativeMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Mat. Amnt (Sales)";
          EstimatePartCumulativeSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Subc. Amnt (Sales)";
          EstimatePartCumulativePlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Plant Amnt (Sales)";
          EstimatePartCumulativeSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sundry Amnt (Sales)";
          EstimatePartCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount";
        END;
        //
        IF PrintAssumptionSeparately THEN BEGIN
          EstimateLineTotal2.COPY(EstimateLineTotal);  //C032753
          EstimateLineTotal2.SETFILTER("Line Status", LineStatusFilter);
          IF EstimateLineTotal2.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            EstimatePartAssumption := 0;
            EstimatePartCumulativeAssumption := 0;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
              EstimateLineTotal2.CALCSUMS("Calc. Cost Amount", "Calc. Cum. Cost Amount");
              EstimatePartAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cost Amount";
              EstimatePartCumulativeAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount";
              //
              EstimatePartAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cost Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cost Amount";
              EstimatePartTotal := (EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cost Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cost Amount") * "Estimate Part".Quantity;
              EstimatePartCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount";
            END;
            IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales THEN BEGIN
              EstimateLineTotal2.CALCSUMS("Calc. Sales Amount", "Calc. Cum. Sales Amount");
              EstimatePartAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Sales Amount";
              EstimatePartCumulativeAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount";
              //
              EstimatePartAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sales Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Sales Amount";
              EstimatePartTotal := (EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sales Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Sales Amount") * "Estimate Part".Quantity;
              EstimatePartCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount";
            END;
          END;
        END;
        //
        IF CurrencyCode <> Estimate."Currency Code" THEN BEGIN
          EstimatePartLabor := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartLabor, FALSE);
          EstimatePartMaterial := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartMaterial, FALSE);
          EstimatePartSubcontracting := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartSubcontracting, FALSE);
          EstimatePartPlant := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartPlant, FALSE);
          EstimatePartSundry := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartSundry, FALSE);
          EstimatePartAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartAmount, FALSE);
          EstimatePartTotal := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartTotal, FALSE);
          //
          EstimatePartCumulativeLabor := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartCumulativeLabor, FALSE);
          EstimatePartCumulativeMaterial := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartCumulativeMaterial, FALSE);
          EstimatePartCumulativeSubcontracting := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartCumulativeSubcontracting, FALSE);
          EstimatePartCumulativePlant := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartCumulativePlant, FALSE);
          EstimatePartCumulativeSundry := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartCumulativeSundry, FALSE);
          EstimatePartCumulativeTotal := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartCumulativeTotal, FALSE);
          //
          EstimatePartAssumption := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartAssumption, FALSE);
          EstimatePartCumulativeAssumption := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(EstimatePartCumulativeAssumption, FALSE);
        END;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalculateSubEstimateTotals@1100525011();
    VAR
      EstimateLineTotal@1100525000 : Record 11072077;
      EstimateLineTotal2@1100525001 : Record 11072077;
      CurrLevel@1100525004 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      //DP01175
      WITH "Sub-Estimate" DO BEGIN
        //C034086.sn
        InitSubEstimateTotals;
        IF "Cumulative Frequency" = 0 THEN EXIT;
        //C034086.en
        IF FormatSubEstimateChecked = FALSE THEN BEGIN
          FormatManagement.CheckFormat(11,sp1,sp2);  //C063045
          FormatSubEstimateChecked := TRUE;
        END;
        CurrLevel := Level;
        IF (sp1 = 0) AND (CurrLevel = 0) THEN CurrLevel := CurrLevel + 1;
        IF (sp2 = 0) AND (CurrLevel = 1) THEN CurrLevel := CurrLevel + 1;

        EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "Estimate No.");
        CASE CurrLevel OF
          0: EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE("Chapter (Sub-Estimate)", "Sub-Estimate No.");
          1: EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE("Paragraph (Sub-Estimate)", "Sub-Estimate No.");
          2: EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE("Sub-Estimate No.", "Sub-Estimate No.");
        END;
        IF CurrLevel < 2 THEN
          EstimateLineTotal.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", "Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No."));  //C032753
        IF PrintAssumptionSeparately THEN
          EstimateLineTotal.SETFILTER("Line Status", '<>%1', LineStatusFilter);
        IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
          EstimateLineTotal.CALCSUMS(
            "Calc. Hours", "Calc. Cum. Hours",
            "Calc. Labor Amount", "Calc. Cum. Labor Amount",
            "Calc. Material Amount", "Calc. Cum. Material Amount",
            "Calc. Subc. Amount", "Calc. Cum. Subc. Amount",
            "Calc. Plant Amount", "Calc. Cum. Plant Amount",
            "Calc. Sundry Amount", "Calc. Cum. Sundry Amount",
            "Calc. Cost Amount", "Calc. Cum. Cost Amount");
          //
          SubEstimateHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Hours";
          SubEstimateLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Labor Amount";
          SubEstimateMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Material Amount";
          SubEstimateSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Subc. Amount";
          SubEstimatePlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Plant Amount";
          SubEstimateSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sundry Amount";
          SubEstimateAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cost Amount";
          //
          SubEstimateCumulativeHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Hours";
          SubEstimateCumulativeLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Labor Amount";
          SubEstimateCumulativeMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Material Amount";
          SubEstimateCumulativeSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Subc. Amount";
          SubEstimateCumulativePlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Plant Amount";
          SubEstimateCumulativeSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sundry Amount";
          SubEstimateCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount";
        END;
        IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales THEN BEGIN
          EstimateLineTotal.CALCSUMS(
            "Calc. Hours (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Hours (Sales)",
            "Calc. Labor Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Labor Amnt (Sales)",
            "Calc. Material Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Mat. Amnt (Sales)",
            "Calc. Subc. Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Subc. Amnt (Sales)",
            "Calc. Plant Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Plant Amnt (Sales)",
            "Calc. Sundry Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Cum. Sundry Amnt (Sales)",
            "Calc. Sales Amount", "Calc. Cum. Sales Amount");
          //
          SubEstimateHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Hours (Sales)";
          SubEstimateLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Labor Amount (Sales)";
          SubEstimateMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Material Amount (Sales)";
          SubEstimateSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Subc. Amount (Sales)";
          SubEstimatePlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Plant Amount (Sales)";
          SubEstimateSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sundry Amount (Sales)";
          SubEstimateAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sales Amount";
          //
          SubEstimateCumulativeHours := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Hours (Sales)";
          SubEstimateCumulativeLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Labor Amnt (Sales)";
          SubEstimateCumulativeMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Mat. Amnt (Sales)";
          SubEstimateCumulativeSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Subc. Amnt (Sales)";
          SubEstimateCumulativePlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Plant Amnt (Sales)";
          SubEstimateCumulativeSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sundry Amnt (Sales)";
          SubEstimateCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount";
        END;
        //
        IF PrintAssumptionSeparately THEN BEGIN
          EstimateLineTotal2.COPY(EstimateLineTotal);  //C032753
          EstimateLineTotal2.SETFILTER("Line Status", LineStatusFilter);
          IF EstimateLineTotal2.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            SubEstimateAssumption := 0;
            SubEstimateCumulativeAssumption := 0;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
              EstimateLineTotal2.CALCSUMS("Calc. Cost Amount", "Calc. Cum. Cost Amount");
              SubEstimateAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cost Amount";
              SubEstimateCumulativeAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount";
              //
              SubEstimateAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cost Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cost Amount";
              SubEstimateCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount";
            END;
            IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales THEN BEGIN
              EstimateLineTotal2.CALCSUMS("Calc. Sales Amount", "Calc. Cum. Sales Amount");
              SubEstimateAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Sales Amount";
              SubEstimateCumulativeAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount";
              //
              SubEstimateAmount := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sales Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Sales Amount";
              SubEstimateCumulativeTotal := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount";
            END;
          END;
        END;
        //
        IF CurrencyCode <> Estimate."Currency Code" THEN BEGIN
          SubEstimateLabor := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateLabor, FALSE);
          SubEstimateMaterial := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateMaterial, FALSE);
          SubEstimateSubcontracting := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateSubcontracting, FALSE);
          SubEstimatePlant := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimatePlant, FALSE);
          SubEstimateSundry := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateSundry, FALSE);
          SubEstimateAmount := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateAmount, FALSE);
          //
          SubEstimateCumulativeLabor := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateCumulativeLabor, FALSE);
          SubEstimateCumulativeMaterial := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateCumulativeMaterial, FALSE);
          SubEstimateCumulativeSubcontracting := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateCumulativeSubcontracting, FALSE);
          SubEstimateCumulativePlant := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateCumulativePlant, FALSE);
          SubEstimateCumulativeSundry := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateCumulativeSundry, FALSE);
          SubEstimateCumulativeTotal := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateCumulativeTotal, FALSE);
          //
          SubEstimateAssumption := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateAssumption, FALSE);
          SubEstimateCumulativeAssumption := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(SubEstimateCumulativeAssumption, FALSE);
        END;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalculateEstimateTotals@1100525008();
    VAR
      EstimateLineTotal@1100525000 : Record 11072077;
      EstimateLineTotal2@1100525001 : Record 11072077;
    BEGIN
      //DP01175
      WITH Estimate DO BEGIN
        EstimateLineTotal.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", "No.");
        EstimateLineTotal.SETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No.", "Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Sub-Estimate No."));  //C032753
        IF PrintAssumptionSeparately THEN
          EstimateLineTotal.SETFILTER("Line Status", '<>%1', LineStatusFilter);
        IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
          EstimateLineTotal.CALCSUMS("Calc. Labor Amount", "Calc. Material Amount", "Calc. Subc. Amount",
            "Calc. Plant Amount", "Calc. Sundry Amount", "Calc. Cost Amount", "Calc. Cum. Cost Amount");
          TotalLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Labor Amount";
          TotalMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Material Amount";
          TotalSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Subc. Amount";
          TotalPlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Plant Amount";
          TotalSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sundry Amount";
          TotalEstimate := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cost Amount";
          TotalEstimateCumulative := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount";
        END;
        IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales THEN BEGIN
          EstimateLineTotal.CALCSUMS("Calc. Labor Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Material Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Subc. Amount (Sales)",
            "Calc. Plant Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Sundry Amount (Sales)", "Calc. Sales Amount", "Calc. Cum. Sales Amount");
          TotalLabor := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Labor Amount (Sales)";
          TotalMaterial := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Material Amount (Sales)";
          TotalSubcontracting := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Subc. Amount (Sales)";
          TotalPlant := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Plant Amount (Sales)";
          TotalSundry := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sundry Amount (Sales)";
          TotalEstimate := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sales Amount";
          TotalEstimateCumulative := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount";
        END;
        //
        IF PrintAssumptionSeparately THEN BEGIN
          EstimateLineTotal2.COPY(EstimateLineTotal);  //C032753
          EstimateLineTotal2.SETFILTER("Line Status", LineStatusFilter);
          IF EstimateLineTotal2.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            TotalAssumption := 0;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Cost THEN BEGIN
              EstimateLineTotal2.CALCSUMS("Calc. Cost Amount", "Calc. Cum. Cost Amount");
              TotalAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cost Amount";
              TotalEstimate := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cost Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cost Amount";
              TotalEstimateCumulative := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Cost Amount";
            END;
            IF PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales THEN BEGIN
              EstimateLineTotal2.CALCSUMS("Calc. Sales Amount", "Calc. Cum. Sales Amount");
              TotalAssumption := EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Sales Amount";
              TotalEstimate := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Sales Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Sales Amount";
              TotalEstimateCumulative := EstimateLineTotal."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount" + EstimateLineTotal2."Calc. Cum. Sales Amount";
            END;
          END;
        END;
        //
        IF CurrencyCode <> Estimate."Currency Code" THEN BEGIN
          TotalLabor := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(TotalLabor, FALSE);
          TotalMaterial := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(TotalMaterial, FALSE);
          TotalSubcontracting := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(TotalSubcontracting, FALSE);
          TotalPlant := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(TotalPlant, FALSE);
          TotalSundry := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(TotalSundry, FALSE);
          TotalEstimate := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(TotalEstimate, FALSE);
          TotalAssumption := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(TotalAssumption, FALSE);
          TotalEstimateCumulative := ConvertAmountLCYToFCY(TotalEstimateCumulative, FALSE);
        END;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ConvertAmountLCYToFCY@1100528602(IAmount@1100528601 : Decimal;IUsePriceRounding@1100528605 : Boolean) OAmount : Decimal;
    VAR
      Currency@1100528604 : Record 4;
    BEGIN
      //DP01175
      IF CurrencyCode = '' THEN
        EXIT(IAmount);
      OAmount := CurrencyFactor * IAmount;
      IF NOT Currency.GET(CurrencyCode) THEN
        Currency.InitRoundingPrecision;
      IF IUsePriceRounding THEN
        OAmount := ROUND(OAmount, Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision")
      ELSE
        OAmount := ROUND(OAmount, Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      EXIT(OAmount);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetCurrencyFactor@1100528601() : Decimal;
    VAR
      CurrencyExchangeRate@1100528601 : Record 330;
      UseSalesExchange@1100525000 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      //DP01175
      IF CurrencyCode = '' THEN
        EXIT(1);
      UseSalesExchange := (PrintTotalsBasedOn = PrintTotalsBasedOn::Sales);
      EXIT(CurrencyExchangeRate.ExchangeRate(2, Estimate."No.", Estimate."Reference Date (Rate)", CurrencyCode, UseSalesExchange));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE StartProcessEstimate@1100529400();
    VAR
      Estimate@1100529400 : Record 11012151;
      SummarySheet@1100529402 : Record 11012172;
      UpdateMgt@1100529401 : Codeunit 11012229;
    BEGIN
      //C020140
      IF NOT ProcessEstimate THEN EXIT;

      Estimate.SETFILTER("No.", "Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));
      IF Estimate.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          UpdateMgt.UpdateTotals(Estimate."No.", '', '', TRUE);
          IF NOT IgnoreSummary THEN BEGIN
            SummarySheet.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
            SummarySheet.SETFILTER(Summary, SummaryFilter);
            IF SummarySheet.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
              REPEAT
                SummarySheet.CheckAndRefreshSheet;
              UNTIL SummarySheet.NEXT = 0;
            END;
          END;
        UNTIL Estimate.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
      //C034086

      EstimatePartLabor := 0;
      EstimatePartMaterial := 0;

      EstimatePartPlant := 0;
      EstimatePartSundry := 0;
      EstimatePartAmount := 0;
      EstimatePartTotal := 0;
      //
      EstimatePartCumulativeHours := 0;
      EstimatePartCumulativeLabor := 0;
      EstimatePartCumulativeMaterial := 0;
      EstimatePartCumulativeSubcontracting := 0;
      EstimatePartCumulativePlant := 0;
      EstimatePartCumulativeSundry := 0;
      EstimatePartCumulativeTotal := 0;
      //
      EstimatePartAssumption := 0;
      EstimatePartCumulativeAssumption := 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE StartUpdateFullCostPrice@1100528900();
    VAR
      SummarySheetLine@1100528900 : Record 11012171;
      Text100@1100528901 : TextConst 'ENU=Start Time: %1, End Time: %2';
    BEGIN
      //C055105
      Estimate.GET("Estimate Line".GETFILTER("Estimate No."));  //assumed to be 1 estimate in filter
      CurrencyFactor := GetCurrencyFactor;

      DetermineSummarySheet(Estimate, SummarySheet);

      TempSummarySheetLine1.RESET;
      TempSummarySheetLine1.DELETEALL;
      TempSummarySheetLine2.RESET;
      TempSummarySheetLine2.DELETEALL;

      SummarySheetLine.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
      SummarySheetLine.SETRANGE(Summary, SummarySheet.Summary);
      SummarySheetLine.SETFILTER(Amount, '<>%1', 0);
      IF SummarySheetLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          TempSummarySheetLine1 := SummarySheetLine;
          TempSummarySheetLine1.INSERT;
          IF SummarySheetLine."Surcharge Over Row" <> Text000 THEN BEGIN
            TempSummarySheetLine2 := SummarySheetLine;
            TempSummarySheetLine2.INSERT;
          END;
        UNTIL SummarySheetLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EstimateLineTotal.CalculateOfferPrice(Estimate, SummarySheet, "Estimate Line", PrintTotalsBasedOn, ApplyLastCalcSurchFactor);
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      Page break per group is not activated for Group of tablix1. For some strange reason printing does not go right when there are more
      estimate lines then fits on one page. As only 1 estimate will be printed each time, this should not be a problem.

      DP01175: subtotals for estimate parts without lines
      Next functions are moved from report Open Budget to store calculated total in order to count totals
      - DetermineSurchEstLine
      - EstLineInSummarySheetLineFilters
      - SummaryLineInFilter
      - DetermineSurchRcpLine
      - RcptLineInSummarySheetLineFilters
      - DetermineAmountRecipeEstLine
      Main procedure:
      - CalculateOfferPrice
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
